[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A FuzzerSecurityIssue indicates a stack overflow occurring deep inside the Java     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         regular‐expression engine while processing an application‐version string in Apache  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         POI’s XSSF event‐based extractor. The overflow arises during a call to              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mMatcher.find[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m in the handler for the “AppVersion” element, resulting in thousands  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         of nested Pattern.match frames and ultimately exhausting the call stack.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         • Issue                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           The stack overflow is triggered by applying a compiled java.util.regex.Pattern    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0mvia Matcher.find[1m)[0m to the content of an Excel file’s Extended Properties            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “AppVersion” element. The fuzzer repeatedly invokes this code path with crafted     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         input, causing catastrophic backtracking or uncontrolled recursion in the Pattern   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         engine, and blowing the stack.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         • Vulnerability Type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           Classified as a stack‐overflow vulnerability in the regex engine. The issue is    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         labeled “FuzzerSecurityIssue: Stack overflow.”                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         • Observations and Findings                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           – The deepest frames all belong to Pattern.match variants [1m([0mBmpCharProperty, Ques, [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         GroupHead, Loop, GroupTail, Curly, etc.[1m)[0m, indicating the regex is recursing through [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         nested quantifiers or alternations.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           – The overflow recurs over [1;36m3[0m,[1;36m400[0m frames before the crash, demonstrating that the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         regex logic does not have sufficient safeguards against worst‐case backtracking.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           – The crash originates in the SAX‐based XML parsing of the XLSX file:             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         specifically in                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor$ExtendedPropertiesHa [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ndler.handleAppVersion                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             which calls [1;35mMatcher.search[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m [35m/[0m [1;35mfind[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m.                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           – The fuzzer harness [1m([0mPOIXSSFFuzzer → fuzzerTestOneInput[1m)[0m merely drives the code  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         under test and is not itself responsible for the overflow.                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         • Code Areas for Investigation                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m.                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor$ExtendedPropertiesHandle [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         r                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – The regex [1;35mpattern[0m[1m([0ms[1m)[0m used to parse or validate the AppVersion element.       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – The invocation of Pattern.compile or Pattern.matcher [35m/[0m find methods.         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. The specific regular [1;35mexpression[0m[1m([0ms[1m)[0m in XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor that apply  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to application‐version text.                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Any helper methods in ExtendedPropertiesHandler that preprocess or split the   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         version string prior to matching.                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. The SAX callback sequence [1m([0mstartElement, characters, endElement[1m)[0m for           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “AppVersion” to see how text is fed to the regex.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. Dependencies on java.util.regex internals [1m([0me.g., lack of timeouts or recursion [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         limits[1m)[0m.                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Reviewing these areas will give a holistic view of why certain inputs lead to       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         unbounded recursion in the regex engine and point toward mitigating stack           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         exhaustion.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoi-ooxml/src/main/java/org/apache/poi/xssf/extractor/XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjav[0m[1;92ma:520[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m530[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m520[0m[39m:                inAppVersion = false;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m521[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m522[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m523[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m524[0m[39m:        private void [0m[1;35mhandleAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m525[0m[39m:            String appVersionString = [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.toString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m526[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mappVersionString.isEmpty[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m527[0m[39m:                return;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m528[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m529[0m[39m:            Matcher m = [0m[1;35mMAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN.matcher[0m[1;39m([0m[39mappVersionString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m530[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack overflow stems from catastrophic backtracking in the static [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32m([0m[32m-?[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,30[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m*[0m[32m)[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.[0m[32m([0m[32m\\dc?[0m[32m)[0m[32m*[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This uses nested, ambiguous quantifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\d[0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*` and `[0m[1;39m([0m[39m\dc?[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon maliciously long or crafted input cause [0m[1;35mMatcher.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to recurse thousands of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimes before failing.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve Existing Extractor Logic:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still need to extract the “MajorVersion” subgroup [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgroup [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAppVersion text is well-formed.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - For real-world AppVersion strings [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. “[0m[1;36m1.2[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m” or “[0m[1;36m-2021.04[0m[39m”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the new [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern must continue to match and extract the major version.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not change SAX handling, buffer management, or any other part of the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextractor; only the regex and its invocation need adjustment.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Strategy to Eliminate Catastrophic Backtracking:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Rewrite the regex to a non-backtracking form with explicit bound quantifiers [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand optional minor version:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ^[0m[1;39m([0m[39m-?[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39m?:\[0m[1;35m.[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m9[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m?$[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Anchors [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`^` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `$`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m prevent searching for sub-matches inside a long string.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Removing the outer `*` quantifiers avoids repeated, back-and-forth [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Digits are matched directly, no nested grouping.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Optionally guard against overly long AppVersion inputs:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – Define a constant, e.g. `private static final int MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH = [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m100[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – In [0m[1;35mhandleAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, before invoking the regex, check:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mappVersionString.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m skip regex to avoid expensive match on pathological input[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               return;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      – This defends against fuzzers feeding extremely long strings, without [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maffecting normal usage.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. In XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m76[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Replace the existing MAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN declaration[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32m([0m[32m-?[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\d[0m[32m{[0m[32m1,30[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m*[0m[32m)[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.[0m[32m([0m[32m\\dc?[0m[32m)[0m[32m*[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          with[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             private static final Pattern MAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN =[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mPattern.compile[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"^[0m[32m([0m[32m-?[0m[32m[[0m[32m0-9[0m[32m][0m[32m{[0m[32m1,30[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m([0m[32m?:\\.[0m[32m([0m[32m[[0m[32m0-9[0m[32m][0m[32m{[0m[32m1,30[0m[32m}[0m[32m)[0m[32m)[0m[32m?$"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Immediately after that declaration, add:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final int MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH = [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. In [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler.handleAppVersion[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m524[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m533[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Before creating the Matcher, insert:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mappVersionString.length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > MAX_APP_VERSION_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m too long or suspicious; skip version parsing[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 [0m[1;35mappVersionBuffer.setLength[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 return;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - Then proceed with:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             Matcher m = [0m[1;35mMAJOR_VERSION_PATTERN.matcher[0m[1;39m([0m[39mappVersionString[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mm.find[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. No other changes to SAX handlers or test/harness code.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A single, simple pattern with explicit bounds eliminates nested quantifiers, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthus removing the backtracking loops that exhaust the stack.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Anchoring ensures the entire string must match the pattern, making `[0m[1;35mfind[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mequivalent to `[0m[1;35mmatches[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` but safer in performance.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The length guard stops pathological inputs early, preventing any regex work on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhuge or crafted strings, with negligible impact on real AppVersion values.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing unit and integration tests will still see “MajorVersion” for valid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mversion strings and see nothing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno crash[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on invalid or excessively long inputs.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not touch external libraries, test code, harness code, or other regex [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic in the file.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Very long but legitimate version strings [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m chars[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will no longer yield a [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed MajorVersion. Mitigation: pick a threshold that covers all real versions [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m is already extremely generous for version numbers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Anchored pattern means that AppVersion strings containing extra suffixes [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., “[0m[1;36m1.2[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-beta”[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will not match; if needed, extend the pattern to allow [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malphanumerical suffixes—but keep it non-backtracking [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., use `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m\w-[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m50[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexplicit limits and possessive quantifiers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Testing:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing POI unit tests for XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor to ensure normal [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcases still extract correctly.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add quick fuzz tests for AppVersion strings up to [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m chars to confirm no [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack overflow.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify that for invalid or too-long strings, no exception is thrown and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextractor completes gracefully.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
